<h2><a id="user-content-시나리오" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#시나리오"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>시나리오</h2>
<p>건강검진 예약 시스템에서 요구하는 기능/비기능 요구사항은 다음과 같습니다.
사용자가 건강검진 예약 시 결제를 진행하면
검진센터 관리자가 예약을 확정하는 시스템입니다.
사용자는 진행상황을 확인할 수 있고, SMS로도 예약상태가 전송된다.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-기능적-요구사항" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#기능적-요구사항"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>기능적 요구사항</h4>
<ol>
<li>고객이 원하는 일자를 선택하고 예약한다.</li>
<li>고객이 결제를 진행한다.</li>
<li>예약이 신청 되면 신청내역이 검진센터에 전달된다.</li>
<li>검진센터 관리자가 신청내역을 확인하여 예약을 확정한다.</li>
<li>고객이 예약을 취소할 수 있다.</li>
<li>예약이 취소 되면 검진 예약이 취소 된다.</li>
<li>예약이 취소 되면 결제도 취소된다.</li>
<li>고객이 예약 취소를 하면 예약 정보는 삭제 상태로 갱신 된다.</li>
<li>고객이 예약 진행상태를 원할 때마다 조회한다.</li>
<li>예약 상태가 변경되면 SMS로 알림이 발송된다.</li>
</ol>
<h4><a id="user-content-비-기능적-요구사항" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#비-기능적-요구사항"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>비 기능적 요구사항</h4>
<ol>
<li>
<p>트랜잭션</p>
<ul>
<li>결제가 되지 않으면 검진예약 신청이 처리되지 않아야 한다. <code>Sync 호출</code></li>
<li>예약이 취소되면 결제도 취소가 되어야 한다. <code>Sync 호출</code></li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>장애격리</p>
<ul>
<li>검진센터관리자 기능이 수행 되지 않더라도 예약은 365일 24시간 받을 수 있어야 한다. <code>Pub/Sub</code></li>
<li>결제 시스템이 과중되면 사용자를 잠시동안 받지 않고 결제를 잠시후에 하도록 유도 한다.
(장애처리)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>성능</p>
<ul>
<li>고객이 예약 확인 상태를 마이페이지에서 확인할 수 있어야 한다. <code>CQRS</code></li>
<li>예약 상태가 바뀔 때 마다 SMS로 알림이 발송되어야 한다.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h1><a id="user-content-분석-설계" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#분석-설계"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>분석 설계</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-event-storming" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#event-storming"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Event Storming</h2>
<h4><a id="user-content-ver1---이벤트도출" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ver1---이벤트도출"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ver1 - 이벤트도출</h4>
<ul>
<li>MSAEZ 툴에서 이벤트스토밍 작업</li>
<li>업무별 담당자를 분배하여 각 도메인별 command,event,aggregate,policy를 도출</li>
<li>이후 java소스로의 컨버전을 고려하여 네이밍을 영문 대문자로 시작하는 것으로 명칭변경 적용
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/mulcung03/AWS3_healthcenter/blob/main/refer/storming_1.JPG"><img src="https://github.com/mulcung03/AWS3_healthcenter/raw/main/refer/storming_1.JPG" alt="ver1" style="max-width:100%;"></a></li>
</ul>
<h4><a id="user-content-ver2---relation정의" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ver2---relation정의"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ver2 - relation정의</h4>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/mulcung03/AWS3_healthcenter/blob/main/refer/storming_2.JPG"><img src="https://github.com/mulcung03/AWS3_healthcenter/raw/main/refer/storming_2.JPG" alt="ver2" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-ver3---attribute생성" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ver3---attribute생성"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>ver3 - attribute생성</h4>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://github.com/mulcung03/AWS3_healthcenter/blob/main/refer/storming_new.JPG"><img src="https://github.com/mulcung03/AWS3_healthcenter/raw/main/refer/storming_new.JPG" alt="final" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-기능-요구사항을-커버하는지-검증" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#기능-요구사항을-커버하는지-검증"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>기능 요구사항을 커버하는지 검증</h3>
<ol>
<li>고객이 원하는 일자를 선택하고 예약한다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>고객이 결제를 진행한다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>예약이 신청 되면 신청내역이 검진센터에 전달된다.   --&gt; O</li>
<li>검진센터 관리자가 신청내역을 확인하여 예약을 확정한다.   --&gt; O</li>
<li>고객이 예약을 취소할 수 있다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>예약이 취소 되면 검진 예약이 취소 된다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>예약이 취소 되면 결제도 취소된다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>고객이 예약 취소를 하면 예약 정보는 삭제 상태로 갱신 된다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>고객이 예약 진행상태를 원할 때마다 조회한다.  --&gt; O</li>
<li>예약 상태가 변경되면 SMS로 알림이 발송된다.  --&gt; O</li>
</ol>
<h3><a id="user-content-비기능-요구사항을-커버하는지-검증" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#비기능-요구사항을-커버하는지-검증"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>비기능 요구사항을 커버하는지 검증</h3>
<ol>
<li>
<p>트랜잭션</p>
<ul>
<li>결제가 되지 않으면 검진예약 신청이 처리되지 않아야 한다. <code>Sync 호출</code> --&gt; O</li>
<li>예약이 취소되면 결제도 취소가 되어야 한다. <code>Sync 호출</code> --&gt; O
==&gt;  Request-Response 방식 처리</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>장애격리</p>
<ul>
<li>검진센터관리자 기능이 수행 되지 않더라도 예약은 365일 24시간 받을 수 있어야 한다. <code>Pub/Sub</code> --&gt; O
==&gt;  Pub/Sub 방식으로 처리(Pub/Sub)</li>
<li>결제 시스템이 과중되면 사용자를 잠시동안 받지 않고 결제를 잠시후에 하도록 유도 한다.
(장애처리)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>성능</p>
<ul>
<li>고객이 예약 확인 상태를 마이페이지에서 확인할 수 있어야 한다. <code>CQRS</code></li>
<li>예약 상태가 바뀔 때 마다 SMS로 알림이 발송되어야 한다.</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ol>
<h2><a id="user-content-구현" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#구현"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>구현</h2>
<p>분석/설계 단계에서 도출된 헥사고날 아키텍처에 따라, 각 BC별로 대변되는 마이크로 서비스들을 스프링부트로 구현.
각 서비스 별로 포트넘버 부여 확인 ( 8081 ~ 8084 )</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-포트넘버-분리" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#포트넘버-분리"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>포트넘버 분리</h3>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="spring:
  profiles: default
  cloud:
    gateway:
      routes:
        - id: order
          uri: http://localhost:8081

            - Path=/orders/** 
        - id: reservation
          uri: http://localhost:8082
          predicates:
            - Path=/reservations/**,/cancellations/**

          uri: http://localhost:8083
          predicates:
            - Path=/paymentHistories/** 
        - id: customer
          uri: http://localhost:8084

            - Path= /mypages/**

<h3><a id="user-content-각-서비스를-수행" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#각-서비스를-수행"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>각 서비스를 수행</h3>

<h2><a id="user-content-ddd-의-적용" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ddd-의-적용"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>DDD 의 적용</h2>
<ul>
<li>각 서비스내에 도출된 핵심 Aggregate Root 객체를 Entity 로 선언하였다:</li>
<li>(예시는 order 마이크로 서비스).</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="package healthcenter;

import javax.persistence.*;
import org.springframework.beans.BeanUtils;

import healthcenter.external.PaymentHistory;

@Entity
@Table(name=&quot;Order_table&quot;)
public class Order {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy=GenerationType.AUTO)
    private Long id;
    private String orderType;
    private Long cardNo;
    private String name;
    private String status;

    @PostPersist
    public void onPostPersist(){
        Ordered ordered = new Ordered();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, ordered);
        ordered.publishAfterCommit();

        //Following code causes dependency to external APIs
        // it is NOT A GOOD PRACTICE. instead, Event-Policy mapping is recommended.

        PaymentHistory payment = new PaymentHistory();
        System.out.println(&quot;this.id() : &quot; + this.id);
        payment.setOrderId(this.id);
        payment.setStatus(&quot;Reservation OK&quot;);
        // mappings goes here
        OrderApplication.applicationContext.getBean(healthcenter.external.PaymentHistoryService.class)
            .pay(payment);


    }

    @PostUpdate
    public void onPostUpdate(){
    	System.out.println(&quot;Order Cancel  !!&quot;);
        OrderCanceled orderCanceled = new OrderCanceled();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, orderCanceled);
        orderCanceled.publishAfterCommit();


    }


    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }
    public String getOrderType() {
        return orderType;
    }

    public void setOrderType(String orderType) {
        this.orderType = orderType;
    }
    public Long getCardNo() {
        return cardNo;
    }

    public void setCardNo(Long cardNo) {
        this.cardNo = cardNo;
    }



    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }
    public String getStatus() {
        return status;
    }

    public void setStatus(String status) {
        this.status = status;
    }

}

"><pre><code>package healthcenter;

import javax.persistence.*;
import org.springframework.beans.BeanUtils;

import healthcenter.external.PaymentHistory;

@Entity
@Table(name="Order_table")
public class Order {

    @Id
    @GeneratedValue(strategy=GenerationType.AUTO)
    private Long id;
    private String orderType;
    private Long cardNo;
    private String name;
    private String status;

    @PostPersist
    public void onPostPersist(){
        Ordered ordered = new Ordered();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, ordered);
        ordered.publishAfterCommit();

        //Following code causes dependency to external APIs
        // it is NOT A GOOD PRACTICE. instead, Event-Policy mapping is recommended.

        PaymentHistory payment = new PaymentHistory();
        System.out.println("this.id() : " + this.id);
        payment.setOrderId(this.id);
        payment.setStatus("Reservation OK");
        // mappings goes here
        OrderApplication.applicationContext.getBean(healthcenter.external.PaymentHistoryService.class)
            .pay(payment);


    }

    @PostUpdate
    public void onPostUpdate(){
    	System.out.println("Order Cancel  !!");
        OrderCanceled orderCanceled = new OrderCanceled();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, orderCanceled);
        orderCanceled.publishAfterCommit();


    }


    public Long getId() {
        return id;
    }

    public void setId(Long id) {
        this.id = id;
    }
    public String getOrderType() {
        return orderType;
    }

    public void setOrderType(String orderType) {
        this.orderType = orderType;
    }
    public Long getCardNo() {
        return cardNo;
    }

    public void setCardNo(Long cardNo) {
        this.cardNo = cardNo;
    }



    public String getName() {
        return name;
    }

    public void setName(String name) {
        this.name = name;
    }
    public String getStatus() {
        return status;
    }

    public void setStatus(String status) {
        this.status = status;
    }

}

</code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>Entity Pattern 과 Repository Pattern 을 적용하여 JPA 를 통하여 다양한 데이터소스 유형 (RDB or NoSQL) 에 대한 별도의 처리가 없도록
데이터 접근 어댑터를 자동 생성하기 위하여 Spring Data REST 의 RestRepository 를 적용하였다</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="package healthcenter;

import org.springframework.data.repository.PagingAndSortingRepository;

public interface OrderRepository extends PagingAndSortingRepository&lt;Order, Long&gt;{
}
"><pre><code>package healthcenter;

}
</code></pre></div>

</ul>

<h2><a id="user-content-동기식-호출-과-fallback-처리" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#동기식-호출-과-fallback-처리"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>동기식 호출 과 Fallback 처리</h2>
<p>분석단계에서의 조건 중 하나로 주문(app)-&gt;결제(pay) 간의 호출은 동기식 일관성을 유지하는 트랜잭션으로 처리하기로 하였다. 호출 프로토콜은 이미 앞서 Rest Repository 에 의해 노출되어있는 REST 서비스를 FeignClient 를 이용하여 호출하도록 한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>결제서비스를 호출하기 위하여 Stub과 (FeignClient) 를 이용하여 Service 대행 인터페이스 (Proxy) 를 구현</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# (app) PaymentService.java

package hotel.external;

import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.FeignClient;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestBody;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMethod;

import java.util.Date;

@FeignClient(name=&quot;payment&quot;, url=&quot;${api.payment.url}&quot;)
public interface PaymentService {

    @RequestMapping(method= RequestMethod.POST, path=&quot;/payments&quot;)
    public void pay(@RequestBody Payment payment);

}
"><pre><code># (app) PaymentService.java

package hotel.external;

import org.springframework.cloud.openfeign.FeignClient;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestBody;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMethod;

import java.util.Date;

@FeignClient(name="payment", url="${api.payment.url}")
public interface PaymentService {

    @RequestMapping(method= RequestMethod.POST, path="/payments")
    public void pay(@RequestBody Payment payment);

}
</code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>주문을 받은 직후(@PostPersist) 결제를 요청하도록 처리</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# Order.java (Entity)

    @PostPersist
    public void onPostPersist(){
        Ordered ordered = new Ordered();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, ordered);
        ordered.publishAfterCommit();

        hotel.external.Payment payment = new hotel.external.Payment();

        AppApplication.applicationContext.getBean(hotel.external.PaymentService.class)
            .pay(payment);

    }
"><pre><code># Order.java (Entity)

    @PostPersist
    public void onPostPersist(){
        Ordered ordered = new Ordered();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, ordered);
        ordered.publishAfterCommit();

        hotel.external.Payment payment = new hotel.external.Payment();

        AppApplication.applicationContext.getBean(hotel.external.PaymentService.class)
            .pay(payment);

    }
</code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>동기식 호출에서는 호출 시간에 따른 타임 커플링이 발생하며, 결제 시스템이 장애가 나면 주문도 못받는다는 것을 확인:</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# 결제 (pay) 서비스를 잠시 내려놓음 (ctrl+c)

<h2><a id="user-content-비동기식-호출--시간적-디커플링--장애격리--최종-eventual-일관성-테스트" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#비동기식-호출--시간적-디커플링--장애격리--최종-eventual-일관성-테스트"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>비동기식 호출 / 시간적 디커플링 / 장애격리 / 최종 (Eventual) 일관성 테스트</h2>
<p>결제가 이루어진 후에 센터예약 시스템으로 이를 알려주는 행위는 동기식이 아니라 비 동기식으로 처리하여
예약 시스템의 처리를 위하여 결제주문이 블로킹 되지 않도록 처리</p>
<ul>
<li>이를 위하여 결제이력에 기록을 남긴 후에 곧바로 결제승인이 되었다는 도메인 이벤트를 카프카로 송출한다(Publish)</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="#Payment.java

package hotel;

import javax.persistence.*;
import org.springframework.beans.BeanUtils;
import java.util.List;

@Entity
@Table(name=&quot;Payment_table&quot;)
public class Payment {

...

@PostPersist
    public void onPostPersist(){
        PayApproved payApproved = new PayApproved();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, payApproved);
        payApproved.publishAfterCommit();
    }
"><pre><code>#Payment.java

package hotel;

import javax.persistence.*;
import org.springframework.beans.BeanUtils;
import java.util.List;

@Entity
@Table(name="Payment_table")
public class Payment {

...

@PostPersist
    public void onPostPersist(){
        PayApproved payApproved = new PayApproved();
        BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, payApproved);
        payApproved.publishAfterCommit();
    }
</code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>호텔 서비스에서는 결제승인 이벤트에 대해서 이를 수신하여 자신의 정책을 처리하도록 PolicyHandler 를 구현한다.</li>
<li>카톡/이메일 등으로 호텔은 노티를 받고, 예약 상황을 확인 하고, 최종 예약 상태를 UI에 입력할테니, 우선 예약정보를 DB에 받아놓은 후, 이후 처리는 해당 Aggregate 내에서 하면 되겠다.</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# PolicyHandler.java

package hotel;

import hotel.config.kafka.KafkaProcessor;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.cloud.stream.annotation.StreamListener;
import org.springframework.messaging.handler.annotation.Payload;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

@Service
public class PolicyHandler{
    @StreamListener(KafkaProcessor.INPUT)
    public void onStringEventListener(@Payload String eventString){

    }

    @Autowired
    ReservationRepository reservationRepository;

    @StreamListener(KafkaProcessor.INPUT)
    public void wheneverPayApproved_(@Payload PayApproved payApproved){

        if(payApproved.isMe()){
            System.out.println(&quot;##### listener  : &quot; + payApproved.toJson());
            // 결제 승인 되었으니 호텔에 예약 확인 하라고 카톡 알림 처리 필요
            Reservation reservation = new Reservation();
            reservation.setOrderId(payApproved.getOrderId());
            reservation.setStatus(&quot;Confirming reservation&quot;);

            reservationRepository.save(reservation);
        }
    }

}
"><pre><code># PolicyHandler.java

package hotel;

import hotel.config.kafka.KafkaProcessor;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.DeserializationFeature;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.cloud.stream.annotation.StreamListener;
import org.springframework.messaging.handler.annotation.Payload;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;

@Service
public class PolicyHandler{
    @StreamListener(KafkaProcessor.INPUT)
    public void onStringEventListener(@Payload String eventString){

    }

    @Autowired
    ReservationRepository reservationRepository;

    @StreamListener(KafkaProcessor.INPUT)
    public void wheneverPayApproved_(@Payload PayApproved payApproved){

        if(payApproved.isMe()){
            System.out.println("##### listener  : " + payApproved.toJson());
            // 결제 승인 되었으니 호텔에 예약 확인 하라고 카톡 알림 처리 필요
            Reservation reservation = new Reservation();
            reservation.setOrderId(payApproved.getOrderId());
            reservation.setStatus("Confirming reservation");

            reservationRepository.save(reservation);
        }
    }

}
</code></pre></div>
<p>예약시스템은 주문/결제와 완전히 분리되어있으며, 이벤트 수신에 따라 처리되기 때문에, 예약시스템이 유지보수로 인해 잠시 내려간 상태라도 예약 주문을 받는데 문제가 없어야 한다.</p>

<h2><a id="user-content-api-게이트웨이gateway" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#api-게이트웨이gateway"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>API 게이트웨이(gateway)</h2>

server:
  port: 8080

---

spring:
  profiles: default
  cloud:
    gateway:
      routes:
        - id: order
          uri: http://localhost:8081
          predicates:
            - Path=/orders/** 
        - id: reservation
          uri: http://localhost:8082
          predicates:
            - Path=/reservations/**,/cancellations/** 
        - id: payment
          uri: http://localhost:8083
          predicates:
            - Path=/paymentHistories/** 
        - id: customer
          uri: http://localhost:8084
          predicates:
            - Path= /mypages/**
      globalcors:
        corsConfigurations:
          '[/**]':
            allowedOrigins:
              - &quot;*&quot;
            allowedMethods:
              - &quot;*&quot;
            allowedHeaders:
              - &quot;*&quot;
            allowCredentials: true


---

<h1><a id="user-content-운영" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#운영"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>운영</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-cicd-설정" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#cicd-설정"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>CI/CD 설정</h2>
<ul>
<li>환경변수 준비</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary>환경변수 설정 접기/펼치기</summary>
AWS_ACCOUNT_ID KUBE URL : EKS -&gt; 클러스터 -&gt; 구성 "세부정보"의 "API 엔드포인트 URL" CodeBuild 와 EKS 연결
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="1. eks-admin-service-account.yaml 파일 생성하여 sa 생성
apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
metadata:
  name: eks-admin
  namespace: kube-system
  
2. kubectl apply -f eks-admin-service-account.yaml
혹은, 바로 적용도 가능함
cat &lt;&lt;EOF | kubectl apply -f -
apiVersion: v1
kind: ServiceAccount
metadata:
  name: eks-admin
  namespace: kube-system
EOF

3. eks-admin-cluster-role-binding.yaml 파일 생성하여 롤바인딩
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1beta1
kind: ClusterRoleBinding
metadata:
  name: eks-admin
roleRef:
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
  kind: ClusterRole
  name: cluster-admin
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: eks-admin
  namespace: kube-system
  
4. kubectl apply -f eks-admin-cluster-role-binding.yaml
혹은, 바로 적용도 가능함
cat &lt;&lt;EOF | kubectl apply -f -
apiVersion: rbac.authorization.k8s.io/v1beta1
kind: ClusterRoleBinding
metadata:
  name: eks-admin
roleRef:
  apiGroup: rbac.authorization.k8s.io
  kind: ClusterRole
  name: cluster-admin
subjects:
- kind: ServiceAccount
  name: eks-admin
  namespace: kube-system
EOF
"><pre><code>1. eks-admin-service-account.yaml 파일 생성하여 sa 생성

<p>만들어진 eks-admin SA 의 토큰 가져오기
kubectl -n kube-system describe secret $(kubectl -n kube-system get secret | grep eks-admin | awk '{print $1}')
KUBE TOKEN 가져오기
:</p>
<p>Code build와 ECR 연결 정책 설정 : code build -&gt; 빌드 프로젝트 생성
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108522319-0e35a600-7310-11eb-8d63-f32cf0651e0a.png"><img width="1029" src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108522319-0e35a600-7310-11eb-8d63-f32cf0651e0a.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108524004-ed6e5000-7311-11eb-831d-e6fca77ab59e.png"><img width="1029" src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108524004-ed6e5000-7311-11eb-831d-e6fca77ab59e.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108524571-843b0c80-7312-11eb-968a-9d14b182afb8.png"><img width="400" src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108524571-843b0c80-7312-11eb-968a-9d14b182afb8.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<p>그리고 다시 뒷 내용은 "3. CICD-Pipeline_AWS_v2" pdf 자료 39페이지부터 (이미지가 많은 관계로, buildspec.yml 작성하기)</p>
<p>환경 변수<br>
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108938749-fce3f500-7693-11eb-8fca-8090f2527dfa.png"><img width="600" src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108938749-fce3f500-7693-11eb-8fca-8090f2527dfa.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>

<p>Codebuild cache 적용 : CICD PDF p.45, S3 만들고 설정해야 함
buildspec.yml에 aws eks --region $AWS_DEFAULT_REGION update-kubeconfig --name $_EKS 이거 넣어줘야 하는데 권한 에러 날 경우</p>
<p><a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/56011492/accessdeniedexception-creating-eks-cluster-user-is-not-authorized-to-perform" rel="nofollow">https://stackoverflow.com/questions/56011492/accessdeniedexception-creating-eks-cluster-user-is-not-authorized-to-perform</a> 상세 내용은 buildspec.yml과 코드빌드의 환경변수 확인하면 됨</p>
</details>
<ul>
<li>CI/CD 적용 및 빌드 성공 결과</li>
</ul>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108810818-5219fb00-75ef-11eb-9fe4-9ae4e2a4e8d7.png"><img width="700" src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108810818-5219fb00-75ef-11eb-9fe4-9ae4e2a4e8d7.png" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
- Buildspec.yml
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="version: 0.2

env: 
  variables:
    _PROJECT_NAME: &quot;teamtwohotel2-order&quot;
    _DIR_NAME: &quot;order&quot;
    _EKS: &quot;teamtwohotel2&quot;
    _NAMESPACE: &quot;teamtwohotel&quot;

phases:
  install:
    runtime-versions:
      java: openjdk8
      docker: 18
    commands:
  pre_build:
    commands:
      - echo Logging in to Amazon ECR...
      - echo $_PROJECT_NAME
      - echo $AWS_ACCOUNT_ID
      - echo $AWS_DEFAULT_REGION
      - echo $CODEBUILD_RESOLVED_SOURCE_VERSION
      - echo start command
      - $(aws ecr get-login --no-include-email --region $AWS_DEFAULT_REGION)
  build:
    commands:
      - echo Build started on `date`
      - echo Building the Docker image...
      - cd $_DIR_NAME &amp;&amp; mvn package -Dmaven.test.skip=true
      - ls -al
      - pwd
      - docker build -t $AWS_ACCOUNT_ID.dkr.ecr.$AWS_DEFAULT_REGION.amazonaws.com/$_PROJECT_NAME:$IMAGE_TAG .
  post_build:
    commands:
      - echo Pushing the Docker image...
      - docker push $AWS_ACCOUNT_ID.dkr.ecr.$AWS_DEFAULT_REGION.amazonaws.com/$_PROJECT_NAME:$IMAGE_TAG
      - echo connect kubectl
      - kubectl config set-cluster k8s --server=&quot;$KUBE_URL&quot; --insecure-skip-tls-verify=true
      - kubectl config set-credentials admin --token=&quot;$KUBE_TOKEN&quot;
      - kubectl config set-context default --cluster=k8s --user=admin
      - kubectl config use-context default
      - |
          cat &lt;&lt;EOF | kubectl apply -f -
          apiVersion: v1
          kind: Service
          metadata:
            name: $_DIR_NAME
            namespace: $_NAMESPACE
            labels:
              app: $_DIR_NAME
          spec:
            ports:
              - port: 8080
                targetPort: 8080
            selector:
              app: $_DIR_NAME
          EOF
      - |
          cat  &lt;&lt;EOF | kubectl apply -f -
          apiVersion: apps/v1
          kind: Deployment
          metadata:
            name: $_DIR_NAME
            namespace: $_NAMESPACE
            labels:
              app: $_DIR_NAME
          spec:
            replicas: 1
            selector:
              matchLabels:
                app: $_DIR_NAME
            template:
              metadata:
                labels:
                  app: $_DIR_NAME
              spec:
                containers:
                  - name: $_DIR_NAME
                    image: $AWS_ACCOUNT_ID.dkr.ecr.$AWS_DEFAULT_REGION.amazonaws.com/$_PROJECT_NAME:$IMAGE_TAG
                    imagePullPolicy: Always
                    ports:
                      - containerPort: 8080
                    readinessProbe:
                      httpGet:
                        path: /actuator/health
                        port: 8080
                      initialDelaySeconds: 10
                      timeoutSeconds: 2
                      periodSeconds: 5
                      failureThreshold: 10
                    livenessProbe:
                      httpGet:
                        path: /actuator/health
                        port: 8080
                      initialDelaySeconds: 120
                      timeoutSeconds: 2
                      periodSeconds: 5
                      failureThreshold: 5
          EOF
cache:
  paths:
    - '/root/.m2/**/*'

<h2><a id="user-content-동기식-호출--서킷-브레이킹--장애격리" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#동기식-호출--서킷-브레이킹--장애격리"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>동기식 호출 / 서킷 브레이킹 / 장애격리</h2>
<ul>
<li>서킷 브레이킹 프레임워크의 선택: Spring FeignClient + Hystrix 옵션을 사용하여 구현함</li>
</ul>
<p>시나리오는 단말앱(app)--&gt;결제(pay) 시의 연결을 RESTful Request/Response 로 연동하여 구현이 되어있고, 결제 요청이 과도할 경우 CB 를 통하여 장애격리.</p>
<ul>
<li>Hystrix 를 설정:  요청처리 쓰레드에서 처리시간이 610 밀리가 넘어서기 시작하여 어느정도 유지되면 CB 회로가 닫히도록 (요청을 빠르게 실패처리, 차단) 설정</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# app 서비스, application.yml

feign:
  hystrix:
    enabled: true

# To set thread isolation to SEMAPHORE
#hystrix:
#  command:
#    default:
#      execution:
#        isolation:
#          strategy: SEMAPHORE

hystrix:
  command:
    # 전역설정
    default:
      execution.isolation.thread.timeoutInMilliseconds: 610

"><pre><code># app 서비스, application.yml

feign:
  hystrix:
    enabled: true

# To set thread isolation to SEMAPHORE
#hystrix:
#  command:
#    default:
#      execution:
#        isolation:
#          strategy: SEMAPHORE

hystrix:
  command:
    # 전역설정
    default:
      execution.isolation.thread.timeoutInMilliseconds: 610

</code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>피호출 서비스(결제:pay) 의 임의 부하 처리 - 400 밀리에서 증감 220 밀리 정도 왔다갔다 하게</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# (pay) Payment.java (Entity)

    @PrePersist
    public void onPrePersist(){

        if(&quot;cancle&quot;.equals(payMethod)) {
            // 예시 푸드 딜리버리처럼 행위 필드를 하나 더 추가 하려다가 payMethod에 cancle 들어오면 취소 요청인 것으로 정의
            PayCanceled payCanceled = new PayCanceled();
            BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, payCanceled);
            payCanceled.publish();
        } else {
            PayApproved payApproved = new PayApproved();
            BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, payApproved);

            // 바로 이벤트를 보내버리면 주문정보가 커밋되기도 전에 예약 상태 변경 이벤트가 발송되어 주문테이블의 상태가 바뀌지 않을 수 있다.
            // TX 리스너는 커밋이 완료된 후에 이벤트를 발생하도록 만들어준다.
            TransactionSynchronizationManager.registerSynchronization(new TransactionSynchronizationAdapter() {
                @Override
                public void beforeCommit(boolean readOnly) {
                    payApproved.publish();
                }
            });

            try { // 피호출 서비스(결제:pay) 의 임의 부하 처리 - 400 밀리에서 증감 220 밀리 정도 왔다갔다 하게
                Thread.currentThread().sleep((long) (400 + Math.random() * 220));
            } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }

        }
    }
"><pre><code># (pay) Payment.java (Entity)

    @PrePersist
    public void onPrePersist(){

        if("cancle".equals(payMethod)) {
            // 예시 푸드 딜리버리처럼 행위 필드를 하나 더 추가 하려다가 payMethod에 cancle 들어오면 취소 요청인 것으로 정의
            PayCanceled payCanceled = new PayCanceled();
            BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, payCanceled);
            payCanceled.publish();
        } else {
            PayApproved payApproved = new PayApproved();
            BeanUtils.copyProperties(this, payApproved);

            // 바로 이벤트를 보내버리면 주문정보가 커밋되기도 전에 예약 상태 변경 이벤트가 발송되어 주문테이블의 상태가 바뀌지 않을 수 있다.
            // TX 리스너는 커밋이 완료된 후에 이벤트를 발생하도록 만들어준다.
            TransactionSynchronizationManager.registerSynchronization(new TransactionSynchronizationAdapter() {
                @Override
                public void beforeCommit(boolean readOnly) {
                    payApproved.publish();
                }
            });

            try { // 피호출 서비스(결제:pay) 의 임의 부하 처리 - 400 밀리에서 증감 220 밀리 정도 왔다갔다 하게
                Thread.currentThread().sleep((long) (400 + Math.random() * 220));
            } catch (InterruptedException e) {
                e.printStackTrace();
            }

        }
    }
</code></pre></div>
<ul>
<li>부하테스터 siege 툴을 통한 서킷 브레이커 동작 확인:</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li>동시사용자 100명</li>
<li>60초 동안 실시</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="siege -c100 -t60S -r10 --content-type &quot;application/json&quot; 'http://localhost:8081/orders POST {&quot;hotelId&quot;: &quot;4001&quot;, &quot;roomType&quot;: &quot;standard&quot;}'

<h2><a id="user-content-오토스케일-아웃" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#오토스케일-아웃"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>오토스케일 아웃</h2>
<h4><a id="user-content-사전-작업" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#사전-작업"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>사전 작업</h4>
<ol>
<li>metric server 설치 - kubectl apply -f <a href="https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/metrics-server/releases/download/v0.3.7/components.yaml">https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/metrics-server/releases/download/v0.3.7/components.yaml</a></li>
<li>Resource Request/Limit 설정
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108804593-09f3dc00-75e1-11eb-9505-6d2140b61d00.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108804593-09f3dc00-75e1-11eb-9505-6d2140b61d00.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></li>
<li>HPA 설정 - kubectl autoscale deployment payment --cpu-percent=50 --min=1 --max=10 cpu-percent=50 -n teamtwohotel</li>
</ol>
<p>Pod 들의 요청 대비 평균 CPU 사용율 (여기서는 요청이 200 milli-cores이므로, 모든 Pod의 평균 CPU 사용율이 100 milli-cores(50%)를 넘게되면 HPA 발생)"</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-siege-도구-활용한-부하stress-주기" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#siege-도구-활용한-부하stress-주기"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Siege 도구 활용한 부하(Stress) 주기</h4>
<ol>
<li>siege 설치 - kubectl create -f siege.yaml</li>
<li>siege 접속 - kubectl exec -it siege -- /bin/bash
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108792500-c1c6c080-75c4-11eb-8d9b-718f7c030de3.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108792500-c1c6c080-75c4-11eb-8d9b-718f7c030de3.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></li>
</ol>
<h4><a id="user-content-부하에-따른-오토스케일-아웃-모니터링" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#부하에-따른-오토스케일-아웃-모니터링"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>부하에 따른 오토스케일 아웃 모니터링</h4>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108803415-f4c97e00-75dd-11eb-9fa0-7c01135c551d.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108803415-f4c97e00-75dd-11eb-9fa0-7c01135c551d.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-무정지-배포" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#무정지-배포"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>무정지 배포</h2>
<h4><a id="user-content-무정지-배포-전-replica-3-scale-up" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#무정지-배포-전-replica-3-scale-up"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>무정지 배포 전 replica 3 scale up</h4>

<h4><a id="user-content-readiness-설정" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#readiness-설정"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Readiness 설정</h4>

<h4><a id="user-content-rolling-update" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rolling-update"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Rolling Update</h4>
<p>kubectl set image deploy order order=새로운 이미지 버전
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108797739-461e4100-75cf-11eb-96fc-959f48dc17c0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108797739-461e4100-75cf-11eb-96fc-959f48dc17c0.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h4><a id="user-content-siege로-무중단-확인" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#siege로-무중단-확인"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>siege로 무중단 확인</h4>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108806577-6f49cc00-75e5-11eb-99c8-8904c9995186.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17021291/108806577-6f49cc00-75e5-11eb-99c8-8904c9995186.png" alt="image" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h2><a id="user-content-configmap" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#configmap"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Configmap</h2>
<ul>
<li>
<p>configmap 생성</p>
<blockquote>
<p>kubectl create configmap my-config --from-literal=key1=value1 --from-literal=key2=value2</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p>configmap 정보 가져오기</p>
<blockquote>
<p>kubectl get configmaps my-config -o yaml</p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>
<p>파일로부터 configmap 생성 (configmap.yml 생성)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: customer1
data:
  TEXT1: Customer1_Company
  TEXT2: Welcomes You
  COMPANY: Customer1 Company Technology Pct. Ltd.
"><pre><code>apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: customer1
data:
  TEXT1: Customer1_Company
  TEXT2: Welcomes You
  COMPANY: Customer1 Company Technology Pct. Ltd.
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>kubectl create -f configmap.yml</p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108792601-fd618a80-75c4-11eb-9386-3d8785979309.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108792601-fd618a80-75c4-11eb-9386-3d8785979309.png" alt="configmap" style="max-width:100%;"></a></li>
<li>출력하는 소스는 아래의 secret에서 함께</li>
</ul>
<h2><a id="user-content-secret" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#secret"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Secret</h2>
<ul>
<li>시크릿 생성</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="kubectl create secret generic my-password --from-literal=password=mysqlpassword --namespace teamtwohotel
"><pre><code>kubectl create secret generic my-password --from-literal=password=mysqlpassword --namespace teamtwohotel
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108868200-4f43f800-7639-11eb-8915-1999a695b85b.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108868200-4f43f800-7639-11eb-8915-1999a695b85b.png" alt="secret" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>시크릿 확인</li>
</ul>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="kubectl get secret my-password -o yaml
"><pre><code>kubectl get secret my-password -o yaml
</code></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108868606-b8c40680-7639-11eb-8296-dfc2ad9cb4e0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108868606-b8c40680-7639-11eb-8296-dfc2ad9cb4e0.png" alt="확인" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
</blockquote>
<ul>
<li>시크릿 buildspec.yml
<blockquote>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108870840-dd20e280-763b-11eb-8e55-bfc9dc70e9e0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108870840-dd20e280-763b-11eb-8e55-bfc9dc70e9e0.png" alt="소스" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
</blockquote>
</li>
<li>시크릿 자바 출력
<blockquote>
<p><a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108871144-30933080-763c-11eb-8e76-453348bb7ec0.png"><img src="https://user-images.githubusercontent.com/17754849/108871144-30933080-763c-11eb-8e76-453348bb7ec0.png" alt="결과출력" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
</blockquote>
</li>
</ul>
<h1><a id="user-content-참고" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#참고"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>참고</h1>
<h2><a id="user-content-개발-환경-구성" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#개발-환경-구성"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>개발 환경 구성</h2>
<ol>
<li>
<p>도커 설치
<a href="https://whitepaek.tistory.com/38" rel="nofollow">https://whitepaek.tistory.com/38</a>
위에 가면 도커 관련 명령어들도 있음</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>카프카 설치</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content position-relative" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="https://dev-jj.tistory.com/entry/MAC-Kafka-%EB%A7%A5%EC%97%90-Kafka-%EC%84%A4%EC%B9%98-%ED%95%98%EA%B8%B0-Docker-homebrew-Apache
https://jdm.kr/blog/208
경로 이동 /Users/jinhyeonbak/intensive/kafka_2.12-2.3.0/bin
주키퍼 실행
./zookeeper-server-start.sh ../config/zookeeper.properties &amp;
카프카 broker 실행
./kafka-server-start.sh ../config/server.properties ( 4 ~ 5 는 건너뛰어도 됨 )
카프카 topic 만들기
./kafka-topic.sh --create --zookeeper localhost:2181 --replication-factor 1 --partitions 1 --topic teamtwohotel
카프카 producer 실행
./kafka-console-poducer.sh --broker-list localhost:9092 --topic teamtwohotel
카프카 consumer 실행
./kafka-console-consumer.sh --bootstrap-server localhost:9092 --topic teamtwohotel --from-beginning
카프카 토픽 삭제 ./kafka-topics.sh --zookeeper localhost:2181 --delete --topic DummyTopic
카프카 토픽 리스트 ./kafka-topics.sh --list --zookeeper localhost:2181
카프카가 비정상일 때 sudo lsof -i :2181 한뒤
kill -9 pid 하고 다시 띄워준다
"><pre><code>https://dev-jj.tistory.com/entry/MAC-Kafka-%EB%A7%A5%EC%97%90-Kafka-%EC%84%A4%EC%B9%98-%ED%95%98%EA%B8%B0-Docker-homebrew-Apache
https://jdm.kr/blog/208
경로 이동 /Users/jinhyeonbak/intensive/kafka_2.12-2.3.0/bin
주키퍼 실행
./zookeeper-server-start.sh ../config/zookeeper.properties &amp;
카프카 broker 실행
./kafka-server-start.sh ../config/server.properties ( 4 ~ 5 는 건너뛰어도 됨 )
카프카 topic 만들기
./kafka-topic.sh --create --zookeeper localhost:2181 --replication-factor 1 --partitions 1 --topic teamtwohotel
카프카 producer 실행
./kafka-console-poducer.sh --broker-list localhost:9092 --topic teamtwohotel
카프카 consumer 실행
./kafka-console-consumer.sh --bootstrap-server localhost:9092 --topic teamtwohotel --from-beginning
카프카 토픽 삭제 ./kafka-topics.sh --zookeeper localhost:2181 --delete --topic DummyTopic
카프카 토픽 리스트 ./kafka-topics.sh --list --zookeeper localhost:2181
카프카가 비정상일 때 sudo lsof -i :2181 한뒤
kill -9 pid 하고 다시 띄워준다
</code></pre></div>
<ol start="3">
<li>
<p>httpie 설치</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>aws cli 설치
<a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ko_kr/cli/latest/userguide/install-cliv2-mac.html" rel="nofollow">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ko_kr/cli/latest/userguide/install-cliv2-mac.html</a>
aws configure 로 액세스 ID 등 입력</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>eksctl 설치
<a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ko_kr/eks/latest/userguide/getting-started-eksctl.html" rel="nofollow">https://docs.aws.amazon.com/ko_kr/eks/latest/userguide/getting-started-eksctl.html</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>IAM 생성
<a href="https://www.44bits.io/ko/post/publishing_and_managing_aws_user_access_key" rel="nofollow">https://www.44bits.io/ko/post/publishing_and_managing_aws_user_access_key</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p>eksctl 생성 ( 시간이 좀 걸림 )
클러스터 생성
eksctl create cluster --name admin-eks --version 1.17 --nodegroup-name standard-workers --node-type t3.medium --nodes 4 --nodes-min 1 --nodes-max 4</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Local EKS 클러스터 토큰가져오기 ( CI/CD 할때 필요한건데, 앞에 설정해줘야 할 게 더 있으니 아래 쪽 CI/CD 다시 참고 )
aws eks --region ap-northeast-2 update-kubeconfig --name admin-eks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>아마존 컨테이너 레지스트리
아마존 &gt; ecr (elastic container registry) &gt; ecr 레파지터리 : ECR은 각 배포될 이미지 대상과 이름을 맞춰준다
aws ecr create-repository --repository-name admin-eks --region ap-northeast-2
aws ecr put-image-scanning-configuration --repository-name admin-eks --image-scanning-configuration scanOnPush=true --region ap-northeast-2</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>AWS 컨테이너 레지스트리 로그인
aws ecr get-login-password --region (Region-Code) | docker login --username AWS --password-stdin (Account-Id).dkr.ecr.(Region-Code).amazonaws.com</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>AWS 레지스트리에 도커 이미지 푸시하기 (이건 위에서 한 거랑 좀 겹치는듯)
aws ecr create-repository --repository-name (IMAGE_NAME) --region ap-northeast-2
docker push (Account-Id).dkr.ecr.ap-northeast-2.amazonaws.com/(IMAGE_NAME):latest</p>
</li>
</ol>
</article>
  </div>

    </div>

  </readme-toc>
